from kafka import KafkaProducer
import time

SERVER = 'guilherme.venturini-broker'
PORT = '29092'
TOPIC = 's7projeto'
SERVER_INFO = SERVER + ':' + PORT


producer = KafkaProducer(bootstrap_servers=[SERVER_INFO])

FILE = 'covid.csv'

with open(FILE) as file_in:
    for msg in file_in:
        data = f"COVID, {msg.strip()}"
        
        print(f"Sending covid data: {data}")
        producer.send(TOPIC, value=data.encode('utf-8'), partition=0)
